<td style="width:11%;vertical-align:top"><span style="font-weight:bold">Item&#8201;8.01.</span></td>
<td style="vertical-align:top"><p style=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman;font-weight:bold;text-align:left">Other Events.</p></td></tr> </table><p style="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">On April&#160;22, 2024, JPMorgan Chase&#160;&amp; Co. closed public offerings of (i) $750,000,000 aggregate principal amount of Floating Rate Notes due 2028 (the &#8220;Floating Rate Notes&#8221;), (ii) $2,500,000,000 aggregate principal amount of <span style="white-space:nowrap">Fixed-to-Floating</span> Rate Notes due 2028 (the &#8220;2028 <span style="white-space:nowrap">Fixed-to-Floating</span> Rate Notes&#8221;), (iii) $2,750,000,000 aggregate principal amount of <span style="white-space:nowrap">Fixed-to-Floating</span> Rate Notes due 2030 (the &#8220;2030 <span style="white-space:nowrap">Fixed-to-Floating</span> Rate Notes&#8221;) and (iv) $3,000,000,000 aggregate principal amount of <span style="white-space:nowrap">Fixed-to-Floating</span> Rate Notes due 2035 (together with the Floating Rate Notes, the 2028 <span style="white-space:nowrap">Fixed-to-Floating</span> Rate Notes and the 2030 <span style="white-space:nowrap">Fixed-to-Floating</span> Rate Notes, the &#8220;Notes&#8221;).</p><p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The Notes were registered under the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, pursuant to a registration statement on Form <span style="white-space:nowrap">S-3</span> (File <span style="white-space:nowrap">No.&#160;333-263304),</span> as amended. In connection with these offerings, the legal opinion as to the legality of the Notes is being filed as Exhibit 5.1 to this report.</p><p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>
